                   President of the World Peace Unification Family, Hwang Seon-jo

 Defeating Satan's Stronghold and Building Heaven
 [Prayer]
 May Your providential path be advanced day by day. May this time, when the gathered crowd before You can offer their hearts as one before the Father, be permitted. In the midst of rapidly changing environments of progress and transformation, may the heart that loves You and admires You remain forever fixed, allowing us to show our pride as Your sons and daughters in an unchanging form, like a rock.
 Today is also the day of Gaecheonjeol. It marks the day of over 4,310 years. In October, there are many days commemorated as victory months for the Unification Church. Tomorrow is Cheonseungil, which is also a day to cast aside historical sorrow and raise joyful shouts of celebration. And on the 14th, we are planning to hold a global event centered around such days. Influential figures from the media will gather on the 4th, and young people from all over the world will gather on the 14th. Please remember, Father, that we have a heart that wishes to revive the sad days of history and return results to Heaven as a day of praise for the Father.
 Please protect the footsteps of all the crowds coming and going, and let the hearts of those who stay be filled with deep sentiments that cannot forget Korea and the Unification Church. May there be opportunities for individuals with such hearts, along with those related to them, and with the surrounding souls, to be connected with the Korean spirit and the providential meaning of Korea's future.
 I know that the work starting from here will not stop here. I earnestly hope that new days of origin will arise that can connect with the world, the heavenly world, and Your heart.
 When numerous young people and prominent figures from abroad set foot on this land, even if their cultural backgrounds, living environments, and all circumstances are different, if they can sense and experience the spiritual subjectivity that has dwelled in Korea and feel that Korea has become a point of origin representing Asia, I believe that a tradition that can be proud from Korea's present to its future, and even to our descendants, will remain. Father! I hope You bless such a background and remember Your children gathered here.
 Today marks a new month, a new Sunday. Please personally watch over this place and guide us to a time of blessing that You can permit. As we calm our hearts, may the heart of admiration and longing that can allow Heaven's presence connect through each individual’s heart and spread to the entire nation and world, even to Heaven. I earnestly ask this, and I pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.

[Words]
 So, church leaders have gathered today? Association president! Church leaders? "Yes." 
 The title of today's message is 'Defeating Satan's Stronghold and Building Heaven.' Let's talk about this topic.
 Behind the human world, there is always a connection to religion. 
 Let’s defeat the stronghold of Satan! If that stronghold is not defeated, the ideal of the earthly kingdom cannot be realized. We must understand this. To build the earthly kingdom, we must eliminate Satan's stronghold; that is the content.
 Our Unification Church members have studied the principles, so we know what Satan's true nature is. We understand the relationship between Satan and God. We also know how Satan has historically centered on the Cain lineage today, based on Adam and Eve and human relationships. We understand that this providential rebellion has spread from individuals to families, tribes, nations, and the world stage, extending even to the heavenly world.
 This foundation is not something that was established in one generation; it has been solidified and developed throughout human history, from the fall until now.
 Today, many religious people believe that by following Buddha, Muhammad, or Jesus, they can reach their own ideal world, whether it be heaven or paradise. Humans may not know what they are, but they have a strong attachment to life. No one teaches them, and no one directs them, but they know that their hearts are strongly driven to cross the threshold of death into another world, infinitely rushing toward that world. All humans who have lived in historical times have experienced this, and the 4 billion people living on earth today cannot escape this flow and are struggling with it.
 Therefore, behind the human world today, the issue of religion is an inseparable connection that has woven itself with history and the human world. Even if cultural backgrounds differ, and there are differences in time, environment, regional relationships, or wealth disparities, religion has always been present in that society.
 In this view, even though we are now in a time that proclaims the end of all cultures, we still see that the religious cultural sphere has a significant historical foundation that influences the times and environments. In Korea, we have seen the Buddhist era, the Confucian era, and now the Christian era. Furthermore, the religious forms centered around the three teachings of Buddhism, Confucianism, and Daoism exist among this nation. When we look at this, it is not just that the Korean people are a specific ethnicity or that they have a reverence for heaven. This is because the nature of humanity is drawn from a common foundation, so it cannot be denied that any nation in the world possesses the power of such religion.
 Humans have the nature to desire better things.
 Today, isn't it true for you? As you go to work in the morning, you think, "I hope today is a lucky day, I hope today is a happy day." This is something everyone thinks. Or when a wife sends off her husband to work, she hopes, "Oh, I hope something good happens to my husband today." They wish for better things than yesterday, and for today to be better than yesterday, and for tomorrow to be even better than today, and so on...
 This is undeniable; as our daily lives are closely intertwined, the greater the depth of our emotional stories, the stronger those desires and hopes manifest. When we reflect on this, we cannot deny the conclusion that it is because of the inherent nature of humanity that this is the case. Everyone wants to go to a better place, and wives want to send their husbands there, parents want to send their children there, and beloved children want to go there with their parents. This is an undeniable common attribute of humanity.
 Why is this so? That is the question. Why is this so? Who teaches this, and who manipulates it from behind? We do not know, but whether a thousand years ago, ten thousand years ago, or a thousand or ten thousand years from now, as long as humanity continues to exist, will there ever come a day when this nature can be completely eradicated through revolution or any other action? No, we believe it cannot.
 So, then, what is the endpoint of this goodness? That is the question. Therefore, those who pursue the issues of life in today's human history and long for the ideals of humanity envision a utopian future, speaking of a world of peace and happiness. From there, literature arises, poetry is born, and all laws that judge based on the historical aspects of good and evil, including laws governing a nation, emerge from this.
 Everything is like that.
 Even in today's Republic of Korea, we must develop, and even if the current situation is difficult, we must overcome it for the foundation of hope for tomorrow. From this perspective, the revolution of consciousness is important.
 The higher level of this consciousness revolution is not about being consumed by empty fantasies of future hopes, but about playing a leading role that can inspire the current stage of life with empirical realities. Therefore, we must carry out a revolution of consciousness. Here, everyone must unite. The government and the people must come together. That is necessary.
 What will we do when we unite? Sometimes we must fight against each other. What will we achieve by fighting? We must win. What will we do after winning? The conclusion is the same. We fight to find a better tomorrow. That’s it. Everything is like that. We fight for a better future world... If we were to express this in religious terms, it is to build an earthly paradise that can be better. It is the same.
 Then, where is the limit of what can be good? Today, in the Republic of Korea, is everything okay if it is good from the perspective of the previous regime in 1982? Is that the perfect place where everything is good? No, that is passing. The current government is also in a position where it cannot stop as long as it is seeking tomorrow! To envision the future, we must inspire a pioneering spirit and engage in the struggle of pioneering life to move forward.
 Here, there will inevitably be accompanying pains or trials. If the government and the people deny this trial and do not endure it, no matter how much they revolutionize their consciousness, it will all return to nothing.
 Humans who wish to build heaven on this earth.
 Now, then, what our Unification Church proposes, the so-called Reverend Moon, has become so famous lately... I am not a famous person, I look like this without any charm... I am someone who straightforwardly pokes at the belly of passing ladies and advises them. I do not say, "Oh, you look so beautiful and well-shaped..." Instead, I poke at their belly and say, "What is this? Looking at your face, you seem like a lady from a distinguished family..."
 So, the ideal of the earthly paradise that the Unification Church advocates, has anyone said such delusions only today? This has been said for thousands of years. It has been said for thousands of years, but we cannot rely on such past ideals. The question is how to develop concrete content that can establish this and realize practical ideals... The words are simple. However, this is an extremely difficult issue.
 For this, countless philosophers have dedicated their lives, and many scholars, those who explore knowledge in various fields, those who pursue power, and all who seek wealth and gold have poured their efforts into this. However, they have not reached the desired position... Today, all those who boasted of Western civilization around the world are now exhausted and find themselves in a desperate situation where they must raise their hands and give up unconditionally. In the face of such global circumstances, how can someone like Moon claim to build an earthly paradise? That is not an easy task.
 Today, people have envisioned such utopian ideals and pursued a better tomorrow, yet the rushing history does not open the door of hope for tomorrow to welcome us; rather, it commands us to turn back, closing the iron door of despair. We are in a miserable era.
 Our young ladies and gentlemen may have their hearts swelling, thinking that they will soon have a joint wedding, without any other thoughts. But regardless of how inflated their hearts may be... When we look at the current generation, they already see what a partner is, what a husband is, what a wife is, what parents are, what a nation is, what the world is, and when they look at the earth, there is no hope, and when they look at the sky, there is no hope, and when they look forward, there is no hope, and when they look back, there is no hope. In such times, if they feel drained, they are the most drained. Their eyes are drained, their arms are drained, their ears are drained, their noses are drained, their mouths are drained; everything is drained. They do not even know what the smell is. Now, if someone says, "This is not sweet but sour. The taste you know is wrong!" they will say, "Yes, this is not sweet; it is sour." The time has come when we must accept this as a fact when the claims are strong and confident and have become popular.
 So now, I am trying to gather the media figures, the so-called journalists, and make them into good people one by one, but I do not know if that is a crazy act. Our Unification Church members say, "What about you, teacher? You have suffered all your life to do good for others; what is that?" Someone like Park Gong-seo is struggling financially, and if I had given him 100 million won, he would have been doing rituals day and night... (laughter) That is a valid point. It is a very realistic statement, but that alone does not solve everything. Even if that were the case, I would still hope for more. So, it cannot be helped.
 Now, in such a difficult situation, the term earthly paradise is simple, but the construction of an earthly paradise is an extremely easy statement, right? "No." I did not misspeak. That smart person who says, "Realizing the earthly paradise is easy," must have lost their mind if they keep quiet, but because they questioned it, they become a normal person. Yes, it is easy? "It is difficult." Young ladies, is it easy? "……" This is where Koreans, Easterners differ. In Western society, if you say it straightforwardly, "This is easy," is it true?
Is it true; is this an easy path, right)? Yes? If you say so, then you say no. (Laughter) But this Korean person asks, you know. (Making a face. Laughter) Why do you look to the side? That’s the habit of a weak nation, I tell you, the habit of a weak nation. Oh dear, if you don’t keep an eye on the big and small ones, you’ll be torn apart, and you’ll die from being crushed and split apart.

The Unification Church, which has emerged victorious despite facing numerous oppositions in America.

Now, is building the kingdom of heaven on earth an easy task? “It’s difficult.” That’s something you could answer a hundred times, but it wouldn’t matter. (Laughter) That’s why the conclusion is drawn that Koreans cannot become the leading race of the world. It’s hard to become a leading race. They always watch for cues. (Laughter) Watching the president’s cues, the minister’s cues, the department head’s cues, even the cues of the section chief under them, the agents’ cues; they even try to be cautious while urinating. They try to be cautious while defecating. What’s the difference between that caution and being cautious about poop and pee?

If the person named Moon here had been cautious, I wouldn’t have been criticized today, and the problematic person wouldn’t have existed either. Even when I went to America, this isn’t something I boast about. I went to America, and here comes a guy with a messy hairdo from Asia, claiming to be something great. They don’t even treat a stray dog like that. In this situation, standing in front of the United States, which claims to be the leading country of the world, having extracted all the essence of Western civilization and established a brilliant culture, I say these kids will fail, they will fail. Would that feel good? Our Koreans are living well now, aren’t they? There are many who live well. But when I tell a girl driving a car that this country, where your parents live and where you live, will fail, do you think she would just agree? No matter how much of a woman she is, at that moment, she would kick me and slap me and ask, “Really?” Right, ladies? You have to answer. (Laughter)

Even if they say they are strong, it’s nothing special. If you’re going to fight, you have to fight with the big ones. If you hold on too tightly in a fight, you’ll throw off your clothes and run away. Do you understand? (Laughter) If you’re going to fight with rich people, you might get a few coins, but if you’re going to fight with a poor beggar, you’ll worry that it will become a burden and burn you up, thinking like that.

If you’re going to fight, you have to face the President of the United States; I don’t play silly games, that’s what I think. That’s why I’m confronting President Nixon. If President Nixon had listened to me, things wouldn’t have turned out like this. The situation in America today would have changed.

Also, Carter is the same. I didn’t even want to touch Ford because he was such a dull man. It would bring shame to the country. It’s not that I’m lying; look at Vietnam, the way they are running away… This kid! Even if he’s the president of another country, he’s still a kid. That kid is a kid because he’s walking a path that could ruin the country. I publicly put up a sign and called Carter a kid in an official setting. So, FBI, CIA, report it, as much as you want. In a few days, he becomes an enemy. I judged that it was good for Carter to become an enemy… Looking back now, was it good or not? “It was good.” After all, it turned out well. At that time, I thought, “Oh, that crazy person.” I’m not a crazy person.

After doing this, fighting with whoever, whether it’s the president or Carter… What does Reagan have to do with me? California and Washington are different, you know. This guy is sitting there like a toad, trying to catch flies while claiming to be the president… What can I do about Reagan? If I just sit still, there’s no problem. But sending people to stir things up, what’s the point… In the presidential election, if there’s one unforgettable person in Reagan’s mind, it’s Reverend Moon. Now that Reagan is president, people say it was good, but if Reagan hadn’t become president and Carter had, Reverend Moon would have been completely finished, everything would have been gone. (Laughter)

At that time, all the reports that the Carter administration was contacting came into my hands. If you look at all the directives through the embassy, oh dear, Reverend Moon is Carter’s political enemy, so they told the South Korean government to do everything possible. These kids! I’m not trying to ruin America.

So, why do that? Because I saw that it would become a solid foundation that no one in history could remove in creating a base of evil in the Western world, it had to be shattered. While I’m alive, I have to take action; once I’m dead, it’s hard to do anything. I have to shoot with machine guns or cannons or whatever and blow it all away at once.

How does that feel? Does it feel good or bad? “It feels good.” It feels good? “Yes.” Now you say it feels good and think Reverend Moon did well, but did you feel good back then? My lips turned blue, my ears changed, my nose changed, my mouth changed, and my sense of smell changed, saying, “What the teacher is doing…” (Imitating while speaking. Laughter) I fought alone, alone. Because of this, during the Carter era, I was able to overthrow the liberal environment and attack Fraser. I broke it down and became the origin of the emergence of new conservatism… If it was because of me, the contribution is great.

Reagan becoming a right-wing president was something that the American political world had anticipated within 20 years… It was almost 20 years. They thought it wouldn’t happen. So how much did they rush? That’s why the problem was significant. And until now… Yes, in America, going to America and laying the practical foundation of the Unification Church is extremely easy, amen. Is that right? How is it? “It’s difficult.” How difficult is it? “Extremely.” How extreme is that? (Laughter) Is it as difficult as fasting for 40 days? Let’s measure it once. How much?

Our Unification Church has a few hundred people here? About 800? If we were to offer a sacrificial offering for 800 people, like the old days when we offered burnt offerings, with firewood, all oak firewood burning fiercely, and skewering 800 people with iron skewers to say, “I offer all this before God, so let God establish this base of the kingdom of heaven in America,” would that work? Can it be done or not? “It can’t.” Then how difficult must that be?

So, having survived until now and coming here to talk to you this morning is a big deal. Is that easy? The media has beaten me so much, as if they were loading me onto a truck… They’ve beaten me for ten years. You need to know that. How much have I been hit? If you were to choose one person who has been most attacked by journalists in history, without a doubt, the American media would choose Reverend Moon. Do you understand?

President Nixon also fled from the presidency in just a year and a half. In just a year and a half. The Washington Post, the New York Times… Reverend Moon has been here for ten years, and now it’s been almost nine years, and I still haven’t fallen off my perch. (Laughter) That’s how tough Koreans are. Koreans are tough. Isn’t that right? That’s why I can play the role of the leader of the Unification Church. (Applause)

Why has Dr. Yoon’s hair turned white? I think God made him that way so that I can use him as material when I speak. So can I take him out? If I had set up Dr. Yoon, I wouldn’t have even greeted him, and he would have slipped away. How is it? Does that sound right? Why don’t you speak honestly once? (Laughter)

The Unification Church members must become the righteous army of the heavenly kingdom that strikes down Satan.

Having small eyes and being observant, being able to look to tomorrow rather than today, and to look ten years ahead rather than this year, that’s what I’m talking about. They are different from others. Everyone has to go up the mountain, but because this path is the closest, even if others say they should go this way, they say, “No, I’ll take a nap and still get there before you.” When asked, “How will you get there?” they say, “Whatever it takes, I’ll get there.” They think they know that there’s a cable car built in the valley beyond that mountain and that they know how to operate it. Let’s ride and float up! They are different. That’s why they are doing this.

How much does the established church in Korea… They think Moon is just dancing around naked and having a good time. I haven’t seen a naked woman dancing. (Laughter) I’ve never even held someone’s wrist to dance. That’s what’s cool. That’s what’s cool.

In today’s world, when an election campaign is underway, they make up things that don’t exist and turn them into accusations, but if there’s someone who claims to unify the world and create a heavenly kingdom, do you think Satan would just sit back? This is the worst of the worst. So, putting on all sorts of hats and letting things flow is the best method. That’s number one.

Even in such circumstances, I haven’t died… Among the established church pastors, I have many enemies. If I hadn’t practiced faith according to my personality, I would have… In the past, among the independence fighters, what kind of righteous army? You know what a righteous army is, right? Yoon Bong-gil killed a Japanese person for that, but Reverend Moon’s righteous army is a bit different. Do you understand? How fierce it is to strike down the historical Satan that permeates heaven and earth with a single bullet. Doesn’t that feel good? Just hearing it is exhilarating. You need to know that it has been so frustrating.

So, what is Reverend Moon? It is the righteous army. What kind of righteous army? The righteous army of the heavenly kingdom, the righteous army for world independence. I see that such words can be described. So, I myself have done nothing. I should have even stolen a bit… To save the country, I’m in the enemy’s camp, and there’s no one who can offer morning and evening sacrifices for me. At that time, I had to go to someone else’s house to get food, and I can’t die on the way. So I need to learn how to steal.

That said, I shouldn’t say such things. (Laughter) Just listen to it today and forget it. That’s just an example. I don’t know whether it’s true or not. So, stealing is like going to a rich neighbor’s melon field and harvesting everything, from the roots to the melons hanging on the flowers, and if you do that, you’ll immediately end up in prison the next day. But if it’s your uncle or cousin’s, that’s a free pass.

So, let’s go to my uncle’s melon field and pull everything out from the roots. Just slide through. In the past, I would tease my uncle, saying, “The young people in this neighborhood really want to eat melons, but you’re too greedy and won’t share, right?” I could read the signs of the rice cake. Since the shape of the rice cake is like that, if the cheeks are like that and the eyes are like that, it means he’s greedy, trying to take even the melon that someone else is eating, so even if a kid is crying to eat a melon, he wouldn’t give even one.

That’s what I’m teaching. “I want to help those kinds of people. Is that bad or good?” If they say, “It’s good,” I ask, “Is it really good?” Then if they say, “It’s good,” I say, “Then I’ll help you,” and that night, I wipe everything out. (Laughter) I take a sack and gather all the neighborhood kids and pull them out. How can I pick everything at night? I tell them to pull it out. (Imitating while speaking. Laughter) I even trained for that. Do you understand? Then what do you know? Do you understand? That’s enough to know, right?

That’s why even if I go to a beggar’s den, I’m a person who has the wit and cleverness to play the role of a merchant. When I go into that world… In this world, if I’m that kind of person, where can I find a place to sit? It’s not easy to sit, stand, and even get food there.

You must become a person who leaves many contributions for the country and the world.

Today, I already knew that this established church, this religious world, would perish. I knew that if I didn’t establish an economic foundation centered on my own hands, leading thousands and tens of thousands and feeding them, and providing a new ideal worldview, the end of religion wouldn’t be far off, so I ran that path. That’s why I have traveled all over the country. But I haven’t been able to go to Mount Kumgang. Why haven’t I been able to go? I had the ability to go, but I couldn’t because I was wandering elsewhere.

I’ve traveled from Jeolla Province to Gangwon Province, Hamgyeong Province; I haven’t missed anywhere. Even to the beggar’s den, all the way to the beggar’s den under the bridge. Even now, standing here, when people praise me as “Reverend Moon” and talk about Korea, it makes me feel bad, but while others feel good, I feel bad. There are many obstacles to what I do.

Ah, now it’s rumored that I have a lot of money. People are coming to hear the words, but they come to borrow money. They stretch out their hands like this… (Imitating while speaking) Isn’t there anyone like that in the academic world? Isn’t there anyone like that in the religious world? Isn’t there anyone like that in the political world? My main business is religion, so how can it work if we talk about money? (Laughter) So, I, Reverend Moon, don’t own a single penny. I feel bad… I have no money right now. I have nothing. I’ve completely handed over all my assets worth about 500 million to the association. I have no money. (Laughter)

Now that I’m becoming more famous, when I sit down, the chaebols come… Now what I want to do is create a global chaebol association. There’s no one else who can do that but me. (Laughter. Applause) There’s no time to talk, so stop clapping and just sit down. (Imitating) That’s probably more enjoyable. That’s something only I can do. Others have been gathering money until now, leaving their wives behind, having affairs, and creating layers of mistresses in the world, doing all sorts of things, but when they come to Reverend Moon to get money, they find nothing. They always follow me. What do they use that for? The way of using it is different.

When I go to America, I intend to use it for America, and when I go to France, I intend to use it for France. I’m going to use it for that region. That’s different. That’s why now, if Reverend Moon is going to do something, there are many people who want to invest. These days, I’m capable of doing what the president of a company like Daewoo does.

I see that something like this, which can question the 40 billion dollars of debt that South Korea has, is coming closer. It’s not that it has happened. It’s coming closer. I don’t know if there are any reporters here. If the sharp-eyed people in the intelligence community report, “Reverend Moon says he will take care of all of South Korea’s debt. Let’s hurry up,” that’s not it. I think it’s coming closer. Do you understand? Close means it’s close within ten years, and when thinking about a plan for ten thousand years, it’s close within a hundred years. People need to speak in a way that can be avoided and can also serve as a shield. That’s fulfilling the responsibility of a leader in an official setting. (Laughter)

So, I’ve created all the capital. Now I’m also going to create a prime minister’s association and a weak nation’s association.
I made a flagpole. So now, in America, they can't ignore me. If they ignore me... it's like a flagpole vendor, you know? Even if there's no designated spot in the market, if there’s no flagpole vendor, the main business won't work either. Do you understand? I may seem like a flagpole vendor in America, but I think that if the flagpole vendor keeps selling cheaply, many market folks will gather around, and even the back end will benefit from it. (laughs) That's how I think.

So, trying to digest all this, my head is old, but when my hair falls out in front of me, I say, "Ah, you worked hard too!" From now on, I think it would be nice to use even one hair to conduct a business. Still, I don't think of it as crazy. Why? Because there’s a lot of history.

Reverend Moon's hair has a lot of history. During the Japanese occupation, I was extorted by collaborators, by police, beaten harshly by the Korean people, and even extorted by women. But this lady here is not one of them. (laughs) I’m trying to put the hair that has been extorted back in place... In that sense, when they say, "You have a lot of stories, don't you?" that one strand of hair has a lot to say.

Even if I say this and conduct a business, there’s no one to oppose it. What is it? There’s no one to oppose it. It could be there or it might not be. So, the members of the Unification Church will all agree that it’s not there, while the citizens of Korea will say, "Oh, what’s that…?" like this.

So, what do I do? What am I trying to do in the shape of a goblin...? The daytime goblin, you see, has a sign attached, and the nighttime goblin runs away when it becomes day, but the daytime goblin doesn’t run away. Ah, it sticks around, attaching signs in front and back, and plays the drum. I did that kind of play in America. Even in this legal battle, I thought of myself as a man representing Asia, a man representing Asia. I’m not a cowardly man like you guys; I’m calm and collected. And I educated many journalists.

What about Reverend Moon? What’s it to me? What kind of court is that American court? It’s a spectator court. I’m someone who fought in the Japanese court, someone who fought in the communist court, someone who fought against the government of Korea. I’ve fought in courts my whole life, so I know it well. Social Issues and the Responsibility of the Media
Respected Chair, distinguished guests, ladies and gentlemen!
I would like to express my heartfelt gratitude to all of you for coming to Korea to attend the 5th World Media Conference.

The World Media Conference was initiated to gather prominent figures from the media to enhance a deep understanding of the responsibility of the media in our society today.

The Korean Peninsula is a microcosm of the world.
The scope of this conference is global, and the understanding we seek to achieve is international. In this sense, I believe it is of greater significance that this conference is being held in Korea, where 32 years ago, during the illegal invasion by the North Korean Communist Party, 21 countries of the free world united to repel that invasion. The united action of these free nations is a noble example of international cooperation, unparalleled in history.

The people of Korea can never forget the grace of many free nations of the world that contributed to the defense of Korea's freedom when our homeland was in crisis during the Korean War, and world peace was threatened. I also find another significant meaning in this conference being held in Korea today. It is the fact that Korea has become a melting pot of various mainstream cultures from around the world.

Korea is a unique country among Asian nations. For the past 5,000 years, Korea has preserved its unique Eastern culture and way of life. In a sense, Korea is where the essence of the purest original Eastern culture is maintained. Additionally, various mainstream religions of the world have entered and flourished in Korea. Today, Christianity, which can be seen as the spiritual core of Western civilization, has deeply rooted itself and is thriving in Korea. In contrast to churches in many parts of the world that are becoming empty, the churches in Korea are filled with prayers and worship day and night.

Korean Christianity can be seen as the fruit of "Hebrew thought," which is the root of Western spiritual civilization. The Christianity that has been evidenced by ancient Hebrew prophets and inherited by Christian saints has become the mainstream religion of the world, rooted in Hebrew thought. On the other hand, in North Korea, north of the demarcation line, the extreme fruit of "Hellenism," which has inherited a tradition opposite to Hebrew thought, is being borne. This is communism, which denies God based on materialistic ideology. These two opposing ideologies are colliding right here in Korea.

The Korean War was a war between these two ideologies. Therefore, the Korean War was not a localized conflict; it was a world war fought between the united communist world and the free nations within the United Nations. Thus, the Korean Peninsula can be seen as a microcosm of the world. All the issues of the world are being manifested in a condensed form on the Korean Peninsula. Therefore, the experiences and successful solutions obtained in Korea are not only solutions to the Korean problem but also solutions to world problems.

So, what kind of solutions are we seeking?
The confrontation between the communist world and the free world is, in a word, a confrontation of ideologies. Furthermore, it is a confrontation of philosophies, and ultimately, a confrontation of doctrines and thoughts. 
If there is a God, then atheism becomes a lie; if there is no God, then materialism becomes the truth. The two opposing doctrines regarding the existence of God cannot both be true. Therefore, it is destined that these two doctrines must collide, and one of them, the true truth, will remain.

For this reason, we who believe in the existence of God must be able to see that God in our daily lives and highlight Him as a God that the world cannot deny. The idea that there is no God can only be overcome by the thorough evidence that there is a God. When this happens, the problem of communism will begin to crumble from its very foundation. The spiritual movement that began with this mission is our unification movement, and there is a logical basis for this movement to have started here in Korea.

Solutions to Social Issues and the Responsibility of the Media
I would like to take this opportunity to briefly explain the background of how I came to initiate the unification movement. When I was 16 years old, I was in North Korea, and at that time, I had a series of profoundly meaningful spiritual experiences. It is very difficult to express in words the experiences I had as a child. In short, the spiritual world suddenly unfolded before me, and I was able to freely communicate with the saints in that spiritual world. In the quiet mountains of North Korea, I had several direct conversations with Jesus Christ. The truths revealed at that time are now the core of the unification principles.

Recently, I testified in a U.S. court that I had met Jesus, Moses, and Buddha. At that time, the world's media was greatly shocked and said it was an unbelievable thing. However, I was simply stating the true facts that I experienced. If there is something I want to proclaim, it is that the spiritual world undeniably exists and that human life is eternal. After having such experiences, I founded the Unification Church, and from that church, the unification movement emerged. This unification movement is an effort to bring solutions to the serious problems facing humanity and the world today.

First, the unification movement actively seeks solutions to the problem of communism. To solve the problem of communism, a new spiritual awakening must arise in the free world. And from this spiritual awakening, solutions to all practical problems of humanity will emerge.

Second, the unification movement is an effort to establish a platform for all religions in the world to cooperate with one another. All religions of the world must unite as forces that believe in one God. The original intention of humanity is to recognize our Creator, who is the Father of humanity. By recognizing one God as the Father of humanity, a unified global family can be realized.

Third, the unification movement is an effort to realize a moral world. This is especially important for today's youth. Today, the absence of absolute moral standards leads to the prevalence of immorality. A culture of greed and selfishness is being fostered, where people do not care about others and seek their own benefit even at the expense of others. If this state continues, our society will ultimately face destruction. To build a good world, absolute moral standards must be based on our Creator God, for He alone is eternal and unchanging. That God is not an abstract concept but must be present in our daily lives. If the virtuous men and women of the world live in constant communion with God, there can be no immorality.

This is a fundamental truth. Lies are bound to be crushed before the truth, and even if those lies are supported by immense economic, political, or social power, they will ultimately not be able to overcome the truth. Even communism, which has immense power, will inevitably face its downfall if its ideology is not based on truth.

As I have developed this unification thought movement, I have faced many misunderstandings from the media around the world. If anyone could feel deeply regretful about the media, I must say that I am in that position. However, rather than feeling resentment towards the media's attacks and seeking revenge, I am rather grateful that the media has shown great interest in me. Of course, I have provided valuable service to journalists. I have given you a lot of material you can use. Following Reverend Moon around, the media has certainly not had the time to feel boredom or fatigue.

In fact, I do not harbor any feelings of hatred towards the media. I firmly believe that there will come a day when the good and infinite potential of the media will be realized. Until now, I have faced many misunderstandings. Those misunderstandings arise from ignorance, and distorted articles come from that ignorance and misunderstanding. Today, my speaking to you in this way is ultimately aimed at enhancing understanding between you and me. I do not wish to avoid the media, and no matter how impossible it may seem, I will do my utmost to convey the truth.

The Purpose of Producing the Movie "O Incheon"
Recently, there has been much controversy surrounding myself and the production of the movie "O Incheon." This movie cost $50 million to produce and involved Hollywood's famous actors. Many people have wondered how a religious leader like Reverend Moon became interested in a Hollywood movie. I would like to explain my reasons.

There are two main reasons I became interested in this movie.
The first is to correct the historical record regarding who the invaders were during the Korean War. For the past 30 years, communists have made relentless efforts to distort the facts of history. Their propaganda has been so effective that many young people today believe that the United States and South Korea were the aggressors who invaded the North. However, the truth is that the North Korean Communist Party, supported by the Soviet Union and China, invaded South Korea. As a result, millions of innocent people became victims of their invasion. This historical fact must be clearly depicted, and the identity of the communist invaders must be accurately recorded. The movie "O Incheon" aims to achieve this purpose.

The second purpose is to pay respect and tribute to General MacArthur's contributions. General MacArthur was a great general who loved God and humanity and accurately understood and despised communism, which is the greatest enemy of humanity and God. In the urgent situation when North Korea invaded in 1950, threatening the survival of Korea and its people, General MacArthur believed that stopping the communist invasion was God's will. In faith in God, he planned and executed the Incheon landing operation, which became a masterpiece of military strategy and led to an impossible situation resulting in a great victory.

General MacArthur was not only a genius of strategy but also an extreme humanitarian. Following Japan's surrender in World War II, General MacArthur became the Supreme Commander over the conquered Japanese Empire. He could have become a tyrant from that position, but instead, he governed the defeated nation of Japan with a fatherly love and mercy.

General MacArthur knew exactly how to lead the Korean War to ultimate victory and what the solution to the problem of communism in Asia was. If the free world had followed his advice and acted upon General MacArthur's will at that time, the tragedy of the divided Korea we see today would not have existed, and there would have been no expansion of communism and countless sacrifices throughout Asia. There would have been no defeat in the Vietnam War that left shame and blemishes on the free world.

I hope that today's youth around the world will come to understand the greatness of General MacArthur. I hope they will elevate General MacArthur as a hero and follow in his footsteps to serve before God and humanity.
I sincerely hope for this.
 Lastly, there is another unforgettable connection for me in making this film. When the Korean War broke out, I was imprisoned in a communist prison in North Korea. I cannot express in words the miserable conditions of that prison. The political prisoners detained there died off within almost six months. Under God's special grace, I endured nearly three long years in that prison. After the Incheon Landing, as the UN forces pushed northward, the desperate communists began executing the political prisoners. My final moment was approaching. However, just a few hours before I was to be dragged out for execution, I was dramatically liberated with the help of the UN forces. This film, "Oh Incheon," can be seen as my expression of gratitude to General MacArthur.
 I never had the chance to meet General MacArthur in person. However, this morning, we are happily joined by Ambassador Douglas MacArthur II, who is the grandnephew of General MacArthur, as our keynote speaker. At this moment, I feel the presence of General MacArthur through Ambassador MacArthur, and it is a great joy to have him with us today.
